LA English
DT Article; Proceedings Paper
CT 10TH SYMP ON ULTRASONIC ELECTRONICS ( USE 89 )
CY NOV 07-09, 1989
CL TOKYO, JAPAN
SP JAPAN SOC APPL PHYS, INST ELECTR INFORMAT & COMMUN ENGINEERS JAPAN, INST ELECT ENGINEERS JAPAN, INST TELEVIS ENGINEERS JAPAN, ACOUST SOC JAPAN, JAPAN SOC ULTRASON MED, JAPAN SOC NON DESTRUCT INSPECT, MARINE ACOUST SOC JAPAN, IEEE, ULTRASON FERROELECT & FREQUENCY CONTROL SOC, TOKYO CHAPTER
HO TOKYO INST TECHNOL
ID DOMAIN INVERSION; LINBO3
AB A ferroelectric inversion layer can be formed in LiTaO3 by proton exchange in benzoic acid melts followed by heat treatment at temperatures just below the Curie point.  This paper presents a method of nondestructively estimating the thickness of the inversion layer by measuring the piezoelectric responses associated with the thickness modes of vibration.  It is demonstrated that the estimated values of inversion layer thickness agree well with those measured by microscope observation of etched cross sections of LiTaO3 plates.
